3a1(1): @#can gdul ba dang / rnam par dag pa'i chos kyis sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul ba yongs su ston pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad yongs su bsgrub par byang
3a2(1): chub sems dpa'i rtse gcig tu smon la btab pas skyil mo krung bcas te 'khod do// byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang 'di lta ste/ chags pa med par spyod pas/ sangs
3a3(1): rgyas kyi ning thams cad du 'gro ba dang / 'di lta ste gnas pa med pa'i lus dang / 'di lta ste gnas pa med pa'i lus dang / 'di lta sde tshad med pa'i lus kyis kun du 'gro ba'i
3a4(1): ye shes kyi lus kyi byin gyis rlabs dang / 'di lnga ste mtha' dang dbus med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phral ba bsam gyis mi khya pa la 'jug pa dang / 'di la
3a5(1): thams cad mkhyen pa'i sgo 'byam klas pa tshad med par gyur pa dang / 'di la sde chos la mi 'jigs par mkhas pa'i snang ba mtha' yas pa dang / 'di la sa phyi ma'i mtha'i brgal pa/ 
3a6(1): mi zad pa'i so so yang dag par rig pa'i tshul bshad pa dang / 'di lta ste gzungs thams cad kyi snang bar byas pa'i ye shes kyi phung po rab tu rgyas pa dang / 'di la ste chos kyi dbying / 
3b1(1): rgyas par gyur pa'i shes rab kyi mig rnam par dag pa'i spobs pa dang / 'di lta ste 'di lta na ma mkha'i dbyings kyis klas par ye shes kyi spyod yul yongs su gnas pa dang / mtshams med cing
3b2(1): mtha' yas pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis spyod pa dang ldan pa rab tu thob par gyur pa dag go// ji ltar gling bani pa 'di dga' ldan gyi gnas su byang chub sems dpa' 'dus par gyur pa de bzhin du/ 
3b3(1): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa dang / dga' ldan gyi gnas dag tu yang byang chub sems dpa'i ming de skad ces bya ba dag 'jig rten gyi khams ming de skad ces bya ba dag
3b4(1): nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan de skad ces bya ba dag gi nam ring na tshangs par smod pa sha stag 'ongs par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis zhabs pus me'i lhang gnyis nas 'od gzer
3b5(1): bye ba khrag khrig brgya phrag stong byung ste/ phyogs bcu thams cad snang bar byas nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad bstan to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag gis 'jig rten gyi kha
3b6(1): de dag gi gleng bzhi pa thams cad dang / dga' ldan gyi gnas thams cad na de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa yod par mthong bar gyur to// byang chub sems dpa' de dag ji snyed kyis
3b7(1): phyogs bcur chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi mthar thug pa dag na/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par rol pa mthong 'gyur ba de dag thams cad de bzhin
3b8(1): gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad kyi sngon byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la dge ba'i rtsa ba'i grogs su gyur pa dag ste/ 'di ltar sangs
4a1(1): rgyas kyi dam par thar pa'i zab mos rnam par 'phrul pa la mos pa shAs ga go/ chos kyi dbyings kyi lus tha dad pa med pa'i rjes su song ba 'jug go// gnas med pa'i sangs/ 
4a2(1): rgyas kyi zhing du 'gro ba'i rjes su song bas rab tu zhugs pa sha stag go// sangs rgyas bsam gyis mi khyab pa blta ba la rjes su gzhol ba sha stag go// chags pa med pa'i sems skad cig gis chos
4a3(1): kyi dbyings khyab par byed pa na sdug go// bsam pa rin po che rdul dang bral ba dang ldan pa sha stag go// brjod du med pa'i sangs rgyas mang po dang 'grogs pa dang ldan dag sdug go// sangs rgyas kyi/ 
4a4(1): byin gyis rlabs grangs med pa dang ldan pa sha stag go// yang dag par spyod pa'i mchog gi pha rol tu phyin pa sha stag go// bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi dran pa rnam par dag
4a5(1): pal gnas pA sha stag go// blo dang sems skad cig thams cad kyis cher 'phags pa rab tu thob pa sha stag go// chu ngur zhugs shing / cher gyur pa'i spyod pa la dbang ba sha stag go// cher gyur/ 
4a6(1): pal zhugs shing chu ngur 'jug pa'i rjes su chud nas ye shes kyis spyod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa sha stag go// de lta bu'i gnas dang sangs rgyas kyi sku'i rang bzhin rjes su rdzogs pa dang / 
4a7(1): de bzhin gshegs pa dang 'grogs shing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang / rin po che sna tshogs ltar grub pa'i lus dang / de bzhin gshegs
4a8(1): par 'gyur ba'i spyod yul thams cad du 'gro ba dang / ye shes chen po'i rgyud kyi sgornam par bye ba dang / ye shes kyi stobs rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan gyi mthu'i mchog thob pa dang / rdo rjer
4b1(1): gcod pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi tshul rab tu thob pa dang / sems cad bye ba khrag khrig brgya phrag stong grangs med pa rnams yongs su smin par gdul barmongs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi
4b2(1): rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad du 'gro ba gdon mi za ba'i mchog thob pa dang / bgrang ba thams cad la mngon par chags pa dang / bgrang ba mngon par bsgrub pa thams cad shin tu bslangs
4b3(1): pa dang / bslang ba'i shes pa thams cad kyi mthar thug cing chos rnam par dgod pa la mkhas pa dang / 'di dag dang gzhan yang yon tar bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa dang / 
4b4(1): yon tan bsngags pa rnam par dag pa mi zad pas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis dus gsum gyi yon tan tshad med pa dang ldan pa sha stag/ de bzhin gshegs pa mngon sum du bya ba
4b5(1): dang sangs rgyas 'byam klas pa thams cad lta ba'i phyir kun nas 'dus par gyur to/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan gyis sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyog/ 
4b6(1): bcur rnam par bltas te de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smraso// yang dag sangs rgyas skye ba med// rgyal ba mya ngan mi 'da' ste// rgyu mthun pa yi smon lam gyis// des ni
4b7(1): rnam par 'phrul par snang // 'di dag chos ni bsam mi khyab// 'di dag sems kyi spyod yul min// gang gis ye shes pha rol phyin// des ni sangs rgyas spyod yul mthong // 
4b8(1): lus 'di yang dag sangs rgyas min// sgra yang de bzhin gshegs pa min// lus dang sgra las gzhan na yang // sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul mi mthong // sngon gyi las rnams ma
5a1(1): gtogs par// rang byung chos kyi spyod yul gyi// mchog gi tshul rnams shes pa ni// blo gzhan rnams kyis mi nus so// yang dag sangs rgyas rnam
5a2(1): 'phrul 'di// gang dag nas kyang ma 'ongs te// gang du'ang 'gro bar mi 'gyur ro// 'di dag rang 'byung sku yin no// rbad med shin tu 'drin pa rnams// chos 'di rab tu
5a3(1): bshad mdzad kyang // chos la gnas pa gang yang med// zhing rnams bye ba kun nas sdang // mkhyen pas mtha' dang dbus med de// chos kun thugs su chud cing rtogs/ 
5a4(1): chos kyi dbyings la rabazhugs nas// rnam par 'phrul pa ston pa mdzad// chos rnams kun la chags pa med// 'gro la de ni bsgribs mi mnga'// tshad med pa yi yon tan gyi/ 
5a5(1): zhing rnams kun na rab tu snang // gang zhig ye shes 'di dag dang // ye shes thams cad rtogs 'dod pas// bsam pa rnam par sbyang byas te// byang chub spyod pa spyad par bya/ 
5a6(1): drang srong rjen po'i byin gyi rlabs// 'di 'dra gang gis mthong gyur cing // de ni the tshom mi byed na// dge ba shes mchog la bsnyen pa yin// de nas byang chub sems dpa'

5a8(1): du med// brjod du yod kyang 'da' bar dka'// tshig gi lam la shin tu 'das// nam mkha' la ni rgyal ba snang // de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin rlabs kyis// me yi seng ge
5b1(1): 'gyur// yang dag sangs rgyas rtog med kyang // rgyal ba rnam par rtog par snang // 'jig rten mgon pos chos nyid dngos// zang mo 'di dag yang dag bstan// gang zag mtshungs pa/ 
5b2(1): med pa yi// des ni sku 'di rab tu 'byung // thams cad gzigs kyi spyod yul gyi// ye shes chen po 'di 'dra ste// 'di la gang zhig rtogs 'dod pa// des ni rgyal ba mngon sum byos// 
5b3(1): yid kyi dbang po rnam dag pas// de bzhin gshegs pa bsnyen bkur zhing // 'di yi tshul las 'da' byed che// nam yang skyo bar mi bya'o// mi zad pa yi bsod nams dang // byang chub
5b4(1): sems kyis bstan pa rnams// the tshom rnam par bzlog byas te// de dag la ni skyo med ltos// rgyal sras gang gis chos dbyings kyis// shin tu bstan pa'i mthar phyin pa/ 
5b5(1): des ni kun gzigs rnam 'phrul pa// 'di dag shin tu 'da' bar bya// dad pa chos 'dis rtsa ba zhes// chos kyi phung po bshad mdzad kyis// dad pa shin tu cher skyed la// byang
5b6(1): chub spyod pa spyad par gyis// sangs rgyas bsti stang gang byed cing // de bzhin gshegs la drin bzo ba// yang dag sangs rgyas dpal ldan las// de dag rgyang mar mi gan so// 
5b7(1): bdag nyid che ba 'di lta bu// gang gis mthos thong mkhas pa rnams// spyod yul thob par cis 'gyur ba'i// sngon lam su zhig spyod mi byed// de nas byang chub sems dpa' dang

6a1(1): mig gis gzugs rnams mthong 'gyur ba// de bzhin sangs rgyas byin rlangs kyis// dag pa'i sems ldan rgyal ba'i mthong // ji ltar brtson 'grus
6a2(1): stobs ldan pa// rgya mtsho la ni 'jug par byed// de bzhin ye shes stobs ldan pas// bsam du med pa'i sangs rgyas mthong // ji ltar sa bon rnam par dag/ zhing bzang la ni
6a3(1): skyer 'gyur ba// de bzhin sems bsam rnam dag la// sangs rgyas chos ni skye bar 'gyur// ji ltar nor gyi phung po yis// dbul ba thams cad spong byed pa// de bzhin sangs
6a4(1): rgyas chos rnams kyis// byang chub sems dpa' rnam dag 'gyur// ji ltar dug tu 'gyur ba la// nad med dug sman rgyal bar byed// de bzhin nyon mongs rnam pa la// rnam

6a8(1): gnas nas g.yo ba mi mnga' bar// sku ni kun du rnam rgya ning // chos kyi dbyings ni ston pa mdzad// ji ltar nam mkha'i khams 'di ni// nam yang rang bzhin mi 'gyur

9b5(1): rnams bcig tsam yang // de ba ni nyid la mi 'jug go// 'di mi 'jig rten 'di rgyal zhes// 'jig rten dgon nam nog yod// gang gis ngo'i ni shes na/ 'jig chen mod de rgyal ba'ang med// 'jig rten
9b6(1): dang par bya ba'i phyir// mgon po dag ni mngon sum sten// de dag gi ni blta ba 'di// shin tu dmigs par mi rung ngo // gang gis chags pa rnam ldog cing // chags pa med la dga' breng ba/ 
9b7(1): chags pa thams cad rnam zlog nas// chags med chos nyid rtogs par 'gyur// sangs rgyas zhes brjod gang yin dang // gang gis rnam 'phrul snang gyur pa'i// chos ni dus gsum thams
9b8(1): cad du// gang gis chos nyid 'di shes shing // gang gis 'di bzhin yid shes na// thams cad mkhyen cing kun gzigs pa'i// de bzhin gshegs par myur du 'gyur// sangs rgyas thams
11a1(1): de bzhin gshegs pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed thams cad kyang mtshan mtshar mthun pa sha stag gis 'di ltar bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang
11a2(1): mdzad 'di'i sngon gyi smon lam dang / sngon gyi byin gyis rlabs dang / khyod kyis ye shes rnam par dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa bas bstan pa'i phyir 'di lta ste/ byang
11a3(1): chub sems dpa'i mi 'jigs pa rnam par dag par bya ba dang / spobs pa chags pa med par bya ba dang / ye shes kyis bsgribs pa med pa'i sar 'jug par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye
11a4(1): shes yangs pa la rab tu 'jug par bya ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba mi zad pa phur sum tshogs par bya ba dang / bsgribs pa med pa'i chos dkar po yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings la sgo gung ras 'du
11a5(1): par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi cho 'phral bstan par bya ba dang / sngon gyi mtha'i mur thug pa'i ye shes dang / dran pa rgyun mi gcod par rnam par dag par bya ba dang / dbang po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin
11a6(1): gyi brlabs par bya ba dang / chos kyi sgo mdza' yas pa bstan par bya ba dang / shes pa kun bzung bar bya dang / 'di lta ste yongs su bsngo ba bcu yongs su rdzogs par bstan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams
11a7(1): cad kyi dge ba'i dra ba gzung bar bya ba dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i tshogs rnams rab tu bstan par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes mi chod par bya ba dang / smon lam chen po'i skabs dbye bar bya
11a8(1): bdang / don shin du bstan pa la 'jug par bya 'a dang / chos kyi dbyings yongs su shes par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dngapa'athams cad kyimi de rab tu dgar bar bya dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi srid pa
11b1(1): slang kya babs pa 'phru pa med pa gra ga de ba nga bshems pa mas cad sa dag par tha bar byang bcar gyi chos sa dang / 
11b2(1): de bzhin gshegs pa'i mthu dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i bsod nams kyis brtan pa dang / gzungs kyi snang ba la zhugs pa dang / sangs
11b3(1): rgyas kyi chos bsgribs pa med pa la zhugs pa dang / chos kyi dbyings snang ba'i chos nyid du bya ba dang / kha nas ma tho ba med pa'i chos dkar po yang dag par bsgrub par bya ba dang / ye shes
11b4(1): kyi spyod yul yangs pa la gnas pa dang // bsgribs pa med pa'i chos snang ba la gnas pas chos bstan pa 'di brjod pa dang / bstan pa'i phyir spobs par gyis shig/ de nas sangs
11b5(1): rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan gyi ye shes tshad med pa'i nye bar bslab pa mdzad do// spobs pa chags pa med pa dang / tshig rab tu dbye
11b6(1): ba la mkhas pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// bsgrib pa med pa'i chos kyi snang ba nye bar bslab pa mdzad do// de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sku dang gcig pa nye bar bsgrub pa
11b7(1): mdzad do// tshad med pa'i dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa nye bar bslab pa mdzad do// byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnam par dbye ba la
11b8(1): mkhas pas nye bar bsgrubs mdzad do// de dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad nyams pa med par yongs su bsngos pa'i ye shes nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// chos thams cad kyi lhag
12a1(1): mthong mngon par bskyed pa la mkhas pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// chos thams cad bstan pa'i gnas rgyun mchod pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do// 
12a2(1): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar ting nge 'dzin 'di nyid kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i gzi brjid kyi phyir ro// de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag phyag g.yas pas/ byang
12a3(1): chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan gyi spyi bo la byug pa mdzad do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje rgyal mtshan la reg ma thag
12a4(1): tu ting nge 'dzin de las rnam par langs to// langs nas kyang byang chub sems dpa' de dag la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam
12a5(1): 'di lta ste/ 'gro ba thams cad khyab par byed pa'i sems can thams cad yongasu skyob pa 'di ni bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' sem
12a6(1): dpa' chen po rnams 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis yongs su sngo ba la slob bo// ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba la slob
12a7(1): par 'gyur ro// da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis yongs su bsngo ba la slob bo// kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi yongasu
12a8(1): bsngo ba gang la bsams te/ de skad du smras pa de dag ni gang / kye rgyal ba'i sras po dag yongs su bsngo ba'i grangs ni du zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag bsngo ba bcu po 'di dag ni 'das pad
12b1(1): mabyon pa dang / nga ltar byung ba'i sangs bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis gsungs so// gsung ngo // gsung bar 'gyur ro// bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sems can rnams kyi 'dun
12b2(1): 'gog cing 'gro ba thams cad yongs su skyob pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba dang po dang / mi phyed pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yod
12b3(1): su bsngo ba gnyis pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad la yang dag par bskyed pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis yongs su bsngo ba gsum pa dang // thams cad du rjes su song ba zhes bya
12b4(1): ba byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis yongs su bsngob bzhi pa dang / bsod nams kyi mdzod mi zad pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba lnga po dang / dge ba'i tshum
12b5(1): thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid kyis rjes su song ba zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo brgyag pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyis rjes su song ba zhes bya ba/ 
12b6(1): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba bdun pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan nyid kyi rang bzhin zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba brgyad
12b7(1): ba dang / chags pa med cing bcings pa dang dkrol ba med pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba dgu pa dang // chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa'i rjes su song ba zhes bya
12b8(1): ba byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis yongs su bsngo ba bcu pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis yongs su bsngo ba bcu po de dag ni 'das pa dang / 
13a1(1): dpa' 'jam dpa' zhes bya ba sha sta ga don 'di nyid brjod de/ gcig na ji lta ba de bzhin thams cad na yang ste/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag kyang sa
13a2(1): so nas slu bar gyur to// 'jig rten kun dang mi ldan zhing // bral bar gyur te dngos med pa'i// yang dag sangs rgyas sus shes pa// de dag mig gi lam mi gnas/ 
13a3(1): shes rab chen po sus mthong zhing // dngos po'i 'du shes mi 'jug la// rnam par bsgoms shing shes 'gyur ba// de dag de bzhin gshegs par 'gyur// 'jig rten la
13a4(1): 'dir long 'gyur te// sangs rgyas che ba nyid dag la// gang gi sems ni mi g.yo ba// de dag mi'i mchog tu 'gyur// sangs rgyas chos la gang gi rnams// mnya
13a5(1): pa'i sems su rab 'jug cing // mi gnyis mngon gyur brtan pa'i rnams// de dag bsam gyis mi khyab 'gyur// gang rnams bdag dang sangs rgyas dag/ rang bzhin pa
13a6(1): par rab gnas shing // mi gnas len pa med pa'i rnams// de dag bde bar gshegs par 'gyur// gzugs dang tshor ba 'du shes dang // rnam par shes dang 'du shes byedapa
13a7(1): da/ grangs med de bzhin shes pa'i rnams// de dag thub pa chen por 'gyur// blta bar bya las 'das pa dang // rnam par blta las de bzhin te// chos la gang ga
13a8(1): rmongs med pa// de dag rab tu 'od byed 'gyur// gang gis shes rab chen po'i rnams// sems bskyed kun la rab gnas shing // thams cad mthong yang skye med pa/ 
13b1(1): de dag grags pa chen por 'gyur// sems can rnams la skye ba med// 'jig pa'ang yod pa ma yin te// de ltar gang gis shes pa ni// de dag blan med par 'gyur// gang nas
13b2(1): gcig pa'ang mang shes shing // bang du'ong gcig dur brtag sa pa/ gnas kyi rnams su'ang byung 'gyur ba// de dag 'jigs pa med par 'gyur// de ngas 'od gter de dag
13b3(1): 'jig rten gyi khams 'di nas 'das te/ shar phyogs su 'jig rten gyi khams 'dacu bcu snang bar byas so// byang shar gyi phyogs mtshams dang / de bzhin du lho phyogs da/ 
13b4(1): nub phyogs dang / byang phyogs su 'jig rten gyi khams bcu bcu snang bar byas// byang shar gyi phyogs mtshams dang / shar lho'i phyogs mtshams dang / lho nub kyi phyogs
13b5(1): mtshams dang / nu bi byang gi phyogs mtshams dang / 'og gi pags dang / steng gi phyogs dag tu yang / 'jig rten gyi khams bcu bcu sngab byas so// 'jig rten
13b6(1): gyi khams re re zhing yang 'dzam bu'i gling bye ba drug brgya'i bar du yang bstan te/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag gi khongasu gang ci yang rung ste/ gtogs par gyur pa dang
13b7(1): thams cad ril gyis bstan to// ji ltar bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi gdan la bzhugs shing / byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed
13b8(1): dang thabs gcig pa de bzhin du/ 'jig rten gyi khams re re dag gi gling bzhi pa bye ba phrag brgya kun na'ang de bzhin gshegs pa bye ba phrag brgya bzhugs par snang ste
14a1(1): thams cad du yang sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcu nas/ byang chub sems dpa' bcu bcu 'ongs par gyur to// byang chub sems dpa' de dag
14a2(1): thams cad kyang ming 'di zhes bya ba dag ste/ 'di ltar 'jam dpal dang / sangs dpal dang / nor dpal dang / rin cen dpal dang / yon tan dpal dang / mig gi dpal dang / 
14a3(1): brtson 'grus dpal dang / chos kyi dpal dang / ye shes dpal dpal dang / bzang po'i dpal zhes bya ba dag go/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang / 'jig
14a4(1): rten gyi khams mang 'di zhes bya ba dag nas 'ongs pa dag ste/ 'di ltar gser gyi mdog dang / yid du 'ong ba'i mdog dang / pad+ma'i mdog dang / tsam+ba ka'i mdog dang / ut+pa
14a5(1): mdog dang / sa le sngam gyi mdog dang / rin po che'i mdog dang / rdo rje'i mdog dang / 'dra ba'i mdog ces bya ba dag nas 'ongs pa'o// byang chub sems dpa' de dag rnams
14a6(1): cad kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan 'di zhes bya ba dag gzhi 'bring na tshangs pa'i spyad pa spyod pa dag ste/ 'di ltar rig byed mi g.yo ba dang / rig byed mi bskyod pa dang / 
14a7(1): rig byed bcings pa med pa dang / rig byed kur spyod pa dang / rig byed bsgrubs pa med pa dang / rig byed mtha' rgal dang / reg byed dam pa dang / rig byed dbang phyug dang
14a8(1): rig byed ngangs pa dang / rig byed pa mas shes bya ba dan so// byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang / byang chub sem su das napa/ byang chub me ma
14b1(1): rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang lhan cig tu phyiran pa dag ste/ gcig ji lta ba de bzhin thams cad do// thams cad na yang byang chub sems
14b2(1): 'jam dpal zhes bya ba sha sug don 'di nyid rjod de/ gcig na ji lta ba de bzhin thams cad ra yod de/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag kyangs so ras smra bar gyur to// 
14b3(1): gos 'gro ba shin tu gces gyur cing // sred pa'i gsal shing ldan par kun shes nas// rang byung kun mkhyen yon tan 'tshal ba'i rnams// de dag chos nyid 'di 'dra 'di yin no// 
14b4(1): chos kyi rang bzhin gnas pa mthong gyur nas// mtha' gnyis gang gang gis rab tu spang gyur cing / ldog pa med cing dgos pa kun shes pa// de dag nga'i 'khor lo mtshungs med
14b5(1): bskor// gang rnams chos dang ldan pa'i bsam pa yis// 'khor ba'i skye dgu kur gyi don gyi phyir/ bskal pa bsam yas rgya chen go gyod pa'i// drang srong chen de'i longs
14b6(1): spyod 'di 'dra'o// gzhan gyis mi 'pham dpa' ba'i rgyal mtshan can// bdud rnams thams cad mthar 'byin mgon po rnams// byams pas gang dag mi 'jigs sgra 'byin
14b7(1): po// de dag chos nyid 'di 'dra 'di yin no// 'di dag nang nas byung ngo zhes bya bar// nyon mongs sel ba'i sems ni skad cig tu// thams cad shes pa su yis rgyu dgyes
14b8(1): pa/ de dag rnam par 'phrul pa 'di dag ston// gang rnams chos kyi rnga ni brdung byed cing // byang chub sems kyang srog chags thams cad la// phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams kun tu

16a4(1): chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal zhes bya bsha sdig don 'di nyid brjod de/ gcig jil ba de bzhid thams cad na yang brjod do// de'i tshetshigs su bcad pa

16b2(1): gzi brjid mtshungs med mnga' la la lo yis// seng ge'i dra ror gsung ba de bzhin mthong // zil gyis mnon ma log gsung mnga' ba// sku'i tha mar su

18a1(1): skyes bu seng ge rnams su rab tu brjod// nang dang phyi zhes bya bar gdags pa rnams// de dag rang bzhin dngos nyid stong pa ste// rtog pa med cing rnam

18a3(1): nga'i tshul ni 'dra'o// zhi ba'i ting 'dzin spyod yul dgyes pa'i rnams// rtse gcig gnyis la'ang skyong pa ma yin te// yid kyis sogs pa de la gang yang med// 
18a4(1): ni sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul mtha' yas// rgyu dang rkyen dang bya ba rnams ngag dang // las kyi rnam smin sems can spyod pa yis// rgyal ba rnams kyi ye shes mi ldag ste/

18a7(1): bsam pa ji 'dra ji bzhin du// thub pa rnams ni de ltar chos kyang stor/ bam po bcu bdun pa/ de nas 'di gzer de dag 'jig rten gyi khams
18a8(1): de dag nas 'das te/ shar phyogs logs su 'jig rten gyi khams stong phrag bcu snang bar byas so// gzhung de bzhin du srang gi phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams stong dral
18b1(1): bcu snang bar bar byas// 'jig rten gyi khams re rer yang 'dzam du'i gling bye ba drag brgya bstan pa nas 'og mir bye ba phrag brgya'i bar du masdud te/ 'jig rter gyi khams de dag ga
